==PAGE:307==
Appendix L
Double Well
L.1
Parameter Convergence
First, a second order expansion around the location of the system ground state was
performed, and the eigenenergies of the resulting harmonic potential were calculated
analytically and compared to the numerically calculated eigenstates, the results of
which are shown in ﬁgure L.1
As before, a series of simulations at varying step sizes were performed. This time,
the total simulated time was chosen to be 1200 [fs] and the amplitude of the perturbing
potential was tuned so the system would end up close to the 60th eigenstate, once
again to ensure that the energies of the actual system will be well below this upper
cutoﬀ. The result of the parametric sweep of the simulation time step for the double
well potential is shown in ﬁgure L.2
Here it can be seen that the system does not require time steps that are quite as
short as in the case of the Morse potential. This is due to the fact that the energy
spacing of the system is smaller and therefore the characteristic resonant frequencies
are lower than those of the OH Morse potential.
The total computational time
required to achieve good results is in general higher due to the longer simulation time.
The optimal time step size was selected to be 0.2 fs, yielding an error of about 0.16%

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

initialization of quantum simulation variables

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%create spacial vector
QMSim.position = linspace(QMSim.minPosition,QMSim.maxPosition+...
QMSim.gobblerBoundary,QMSim.stepsPosition);
QMSim.positionStepSize = QMSim.position(2)-QMSim.position(1);
%calculate eigenfunctions/energies of Morse potential
[QMSim.eigPsi,QMSim.eigEvec] = ...
MorseEigenstates(QMSim.position,QMSim.morsePot);
%create static potential vector, absorbing boundary potential,
%and molecular dipole moment vector
QMSim.potentialV = QMSim.morsePot.De.*...
(exp(-2.*QMSim.morsePot.a.*(QMSim.position-QMSim.morsePot.re))...
-2.*exp(-QMSim.morsePot.a.*...
(QMSim.position-QMSim.morsePot.re)));

==PAGE:320==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
QMSim.absorbingV = -i*heaviside(QMSim.position-QMSim.maxPosition).*...
QMSim.gobblerSlope.*...
(QMSim.position-QMSim.maxPosition).ˆQMSim.gobblerStrength;
QMSim.staticV = QMSim.potentialV + QMSim.absorbingV;
QMSim.molDipole = QMSim.dipoleFactors.mu0.*...
QMSim.position.*exp(-QMSim.position./QMSim.dipoleFactors.r0);
%create initial wave function from the nth eigenstate of the potential well
QMSim.psiInit = QMSim.eigPsi(:,QMSim.levelStart+1);
%convert refracory period to atomic units
QMSim.timeRelax = Pulse.timeRelax/atomicConversion;

2*Pulse.transitionFrequencies(1)];

GAAlg.lBounds = [GAAlg.lBounds,-factor];
GAAlg.uBounds = [GAAlg.uBounds,factor];

ChirpFitness()
%This function evaluates the fitness of a spectral chirp
%for use by the ChirpOptimization script
function [fitness] = ChirpFitness(params,GAAlg,Pulse,Chirp,QMSim)
%construct chirped and/or masked frequency distribution
chirpCoefs = params(2:end);
centralFreq = params(1);
amplitudeFunction = @(omega) sqrt((pi/Pulse.alpha0)).*...
exp(-((omega-centralFreq).ˆ2)./(4*Pulse.alpha0));
frequencyIndexLeft = find(Pulse.frequency >= centralFreq...
- Chirp.regionSize/2,1,’first’);
frequencyIndexRight = find(Pulse.frequency <= centralFreq...
+ Chirp.regionSize/2,1,’last’);
frequencyWindow = Pulse.frequency(frequencyIndexLeft:frequencyIndexRight);
[chirpReduced,maskReduced] = ...
ChirpConstruction(frequencyWindow,centralFreq,chirpCoefs,Chirp);
chirp = [sparse(1,frequencyIndexLeft-1),chirpReduced,...
135
==PAGE:328==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
sparse(1,length(Pulse.frequency)-frequencyIndexRight)];
intensityFreq = [sparse(1,frequencyIndexLeft-1),...
amplitudeFunction(frequencyWindow),...
sparse(1,length(Pulse.frequency)-frequencyIndexRight)];
if strcmp(Chirp.intensityMasking,’true’)
mask = [sparse(1,frequencyIndexLeft-1),maskReduced,...
sparse(1,length(Pulse.frequency)-frequencyIndexRight)];
intensityFreqChirped = intensityFreq.*exp(i*chirp).*mask;
else
intensityFreqChirped = intensityFreq.*exp(i*chirp);
end
%perform fourier transformation of shaped spectral amplitude to
%temporal intensity
[pulseShaped] = Fourier2Time(Pulse.time,intensityFreqChirped);
%evaluate width of transformed pulse
[width,t0] = WidthAnalysis(Pulse.time,pulseShaped);

%convert and interpolate pulse data to atomic time for quantum propagation
[timeAtomic,pulseInterp] = PulseInterpolation(Pulse.time,pulseShaped,...
QMSim.timeStepSize,Pulse.timeRelax);
%create dynamic potential vector, pass to S.O. propagation function,
%and measure exitation level
dynamicV = QMSim.amplitude*real(pulseInterp);
[˜,psiSave,˜] = SplitOperatorPropagation(QMSim.position,timeAtomic,...
QMSim.psiInit,QMSim.staticV,dynamicV,QMSim.molDipole,[],...
QMSim.morsePot.m);
spectral = QMSim.eigPsi’*psiSave*QMSim.positionStepSize;
unbound = (1-sum(abs(spectral(:,1:end)).ˆ2));
if QMSim.levelTarget == -1
state = 1-sum(abs(spectral(:,1:end)).ˆ2);
else
state = abs(spectral(levelTarget+1,1:end)).ˆ2;

==PAGE:330==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
%evaluate pulse fitness, and incur penalties for width and non-centeredness
rightTarget = GAAlg.penaltyBoundaries*GAAlg.maxPulseWidth/2;
leftTarget = -GAAlg.penaltyBoundaries*GAAlg.maxPulseWidth/2;
rightLocation = t0 + width/2;
leftLocation = t0 - width/2;
rightMin = leftLocation + GAAlg.minPulseWidth;
rightMax = leftLocation + GAAlg.maxPulseWidth;
leftMin = rightLocation - GAAlg.maxPulseWidth;
leftMax = rightLocation - GAAlg.minPulseWidth;
if rightMax <= rightTarget
rightPenaltyFunct = @(x) exp((rightTarget-x).*...
(log(GAAlg.penaltyStrength)/(rightTarget-rightMin)).*...
(1-heaviside(x-rightTarget)));
else

(log(GAAlg.penaltyStrength)/(rightTarget-rightMin)).*...
(1-heaviside(x-rightTarget))+...
(x-rightTarget).*(log(GAAlg.penaltyStrength)/...
(rightMax-rightTarget)).*heaviside(x-rightTarget));
138
==PAGE:331==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
end
if leftMax <= leftTarget
leftPenaltyFunct = @(x) exp((leftTarget-x).*...
(log(GAAlg.penaltyStrength)/(leftTarget-leftMin)).*...
(1-heaviside(x-leftTarget)));
else
leftPenaltyFunct = @(x) exp((leftTarget-x).*...
(log(GAAlg.penaltyStrength)/(leftTarget-leftMin)).*...
(1-heaviside(x-leftTarget))+(x-leftTarget).*...
(log(GAAlg.penaltyStrength)/(leftMax-leftTarget)).*...
heaviside(x-leftTarget));
end
penalty = (rightPenaltyFunct(rightLocation)+...
leftPenaltyFunct(leftLocation))/2;
fitness = (penalty/abs(state));
end

%absorbing boundary strength coefficient

M.5
FrequencyFitness()
%Fitness function for frequency optimization script
function [fitness] = FrequencyFitness(params,QMSim,GAAlg)
%if width variation = true, construct the parameters using the total pulse
%energy and width parameters. else, just construct the frequency
%distribution function using the constant amplitude and pulse shape
%parameters.
if strcmp(GAAlg.widthVariation,’true’)
pulseWidth = params(1);
frequencyCenter = params(2);
coefsFreq = params(3:end);
sectionWidth = pulseWidth*sqrt(20/13);
amplitude = sqrt(QMSim.totalEnergy/(pulseWidth*(8/3)*sqrt(20/13)));
coefsEnvelope = [sectionWidth,2*sectionWidth,sectionWidth];
timeEnvelope = sum(coefsEnvelope);
[pulseFunction,˜] = FrequencyFunctionCreation(coefsEnvelope,...
157
==PAGE:350==

coefsFreq,frequencyCenter);

round((timeEnvelope+QMSim.timeRelax)/QMSim.timeStep));
pulse = pulseFunction(time);
dynamicV = amplitude.*real(pulse);
else
frequencyCenter = params(1);
coefsFreq = params(2:end);
[pulseFunction,˜] = FrequencyFunctionCreation(QMSim.coefsEnvelope,...
coefsFreq,frequencyCenter);
time = linspace(0,QMSim.timeEnvelope+QMSim.timeRelax,...

==PAGE:352==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
M.6
FrequencyFunctionCreation()
%creates a trapezoidal pulse of height 1 with a polynomially varying
%frequency. coefsEnvelope has three values for the leading, middle and
%trailing trapezoid edges. coefsFreq is the polynomial coefficients in
%ascending order, and frequencyCenter is the center location in time of the
%polynomial frequency distribution
function [pulseFunction,frequencyInst] =...
FrequencyFunctionCreation(coefsEnvelope,coefsFreq,frequencyCenter)
%extract relevant parameters from variable structure
t0 = frequencyCenter;
t1 = coefsEnvelope(1);
t2 = coefsEnvelope(2);
t3 = coefsEnvelope(3);
%create envelope function
envelopeFunction = @(t) heaviside(t1-t).*(t./t1)+(heaviside(t-t1)-...
heaviside(t-(t1+t2)))+((heaviside(t-(t1+t2))-...
heaviside(t-(t1+t2+t3))).*(1-(t-t1-t2)./t3));
%create frequency function
160
==PAGE:353==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
omegaFunction = @(t) 0;
frequencyInst = @(t) 0;
for n = 1:length(coefsFreq)
omegaFunction = @(t) omegaFunction(t)+...
coefsFreq(n).*((t-t0).ˆ(n-1));
frequencyInst = @(t) frequencyInst(t)+...
(n-1).*coefsFreq(n).*((t-t0).ˆ(n-2));
end
frequencyFunction = @(t) exp(i.*(omegaFunction(t)));
%create pulse function
pulseFunction = @(t) envelopeFunction(t).*frequencyFunction(t);
end

APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
M.7
FrequencyConstraint()
%Nonlinear constraints on the frequency optimazation script
function [constraint,constraintEq] =...
FrequencyConstraint(params,QMSim,GAAlg)
%create instantaneous frequency function for variable or
%non variable widths
if strcmp(GAAlg.widthVariation,’true’)
pulseWidth = params(1);
frequencyCenter = params(2);
coefsFreq = params(3:end);
sectionWidth = pulseWidth*sqrt(20/13);
coefsEnvelope = [sectionWidth,2*sectionWidth,sectionWidth];
timeEnvelope = sum(coefsEnvelope);
[˜,omegaFunction] = FrequencyFunctionCreation(coefsEnvelope,...
coefsFreq,frequencyCenter);
time = linspace(0,timeEnvelope,round((timeEnvelope)/QMSim.timeStep));
162
==PAGE:355==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
else
frequencyCenter = params(1);
coefsFreq = params(2:end);
[˜,omegaFunction] = FrequencyFunctionCreation(QMSim.coefsEnvelope,...
coefsFreq,frequencyCenter);
time = linspace(0,QMSim.timeEnvelope,...
round((QMSim.timeEnvelope)/QMSim.timeStep));
end
energyMax = max(omegaFunction(time)).*QMSim.hbar;
energyMin = min(omegaFunction(time)).*QMSim.hbar;
if length(GAAlg.nonlinearBounds) == 1
constraint = [GAAlg.nonlinearBounds(1) - energyMin];
else
constraint = [energyMax - GAAlg.nonlinearBounds(2);...
GAAlg.nonlinearBounds(1) - energyMin];
end
constraintEq = [];
end

ShapeFitness()
%This function evaluates the fitness of the chirp guesses provided by the
%GA pulse shaping algorithm
function [fitness] = ShapeFitness(params,Target,Pulse,Chirp)
[chirpReduced,maskReduced] = ...
ChirpConstruction(Pulse.frequenciesReduced,...
Pulse.centralFrequency,params,Chirp);
chirp = [sparse(1,Chirp.frequencyIndexLeft-1),...
chirpReduced,sparse(1,length(Pulse.frequencies)...
-Chirp.frequencyIndexRight)];
if strcmp(Target.intensityMasking,’true’)
mask = [sparse(1,Chirp.frequencyIndexLeft-1),...
maskReduced,sparse(1,length(Pulse.frequencies)-...
Chirp.frequencyIndexRight)];
intensityFreqChirped = Pulse.intensityFreq.*exp(1i*chirp).*mask;
else
intensityFreqChirped = Pulse.intensityFreq.*exp(1i*chirp);
175
==PAGE:368==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
end
pulse = Fourier2Time(Pulse.time,intensityFreqChirped);
%divide by pulse intensity to normalize fitness
fitness = trapz(abs(pulse-Target.pulse).ˆ2)/(2*Pulse.intensity)+1;
end

APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
M.10
PulseInterpolation()
%This function interpolates a time dependent potential and converts
%it to atomic time units. use [relaxTime] to add a refractory period
%as a fraction of the interpolated pulse length. stepSize is the length
%of an atomic time step, for most purposes this will be about 2.5
function [time,pulseInterp] =...
PulseInterpolation(timeSeconds,pulse,timeStepSize,relaxTime)
%atomic time conversion factor
timeAtomic = 2.41888432650e-17;
%create interpolated pulse and time vectors
timeSecondsShifted = timeSeconds - timeSeconds(1);
timeAtomicVector = timeSecondsShifted/timeAtomic;
relaxTimeAtomic = relaxTime/timeAtomic;
pulseTimeAtomic = (timeAtomicVector(end)-timeAtomicVector(1));
timeGlobal = pulseTimeAtomic + relaxTimeAtomic;
timeSteps = round(timeGlobal/timeStepSize);
dt = timeGlobal/timeSteps;
time = linspace(0,timeGlobal+dt,timeSteps+1);
pulseIndexEnd = find(time>timeAtomicVector(end),1);
pulseInterp = [spline(timeAtomicVector,pulse,...
time(1:pulseIndexEnd)),zeros(1,timeSteps-pulseIndexEnd+1)];
end

M.11
WignerDistribution()
%This function calculates the numerical wigner distribution matrix
%and outputs a time and frequency vector
function [wignerFreq,wignerTime,wignerDist] =...
WignerDistribution(time,pulse)
pulse = pulse’;
timeLength = time(end)-time(1);
timeSteps = length(time);
N = 2ˆnextpow2(timeSteps);
dt = timeLength/timeSteps;
sampFreq = 1/dt;
tIndex = 1:timeSteps;
pulseLength = length(pulse);
tfr = zeros (N,timeSteps);
for icol=1:timeSteps,
ti= tIndex(icol);
taumax=min([ti-1,pulseLength-ti,round(N/2)-1]);
tau=-taumax:taumax;
indices= rem(N+tau,N)+1;
178
==PAGE:371==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
tfr(indices,icol) = pulse(ti+tau,1) .* conj(pulse(ti-tau,1));
tau=round(N/2);
if (ti<=pulseLength-tau)&(ti>=tau+1),
tfr(tau+1,icol) = 0.5*(pulse(ti+tau,1)*conj(pulse(ti-tau,xcol))...
+pulse(ti-tau,1)*conj(pulse(ti+tau,xcol)));
end
end
tfr = fft(tfr);
tfr = real(tfr);
wignerDist = fftshift(tfr,1);
wignerTime = time;
wignerFreq = linspace(-timeSteps/2,timeSteps/2-1,N)*...
(sampFreq/(2*timeSteps));
end

APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
M.12
Time2Fourier()
%this function transforms a temporal signal into a spectral distribution
%and a corresponding frequency vector in rad
function [frequency,time,amplitude] = ...
Time2Fourier(timeTotal,sampleFrequency,pulseFunction)
T = timeTotal;
N = round(timeTotal*sampleFrequency);
dt = T/N;
fs = 1/dt;
df = fs/N;
if mod(N,2) == 0;
time = linspace(-T/2,T/2-dt,N);
frequency = 2*pi*linspace((-fs/2),(fs/2-df),N);
else
time = linspace(-(T-dt)/2,(T-dt)/2,N);
frequency = 2*pi*linspace((-(fs-df)/2),((fs-df)/2),N);
end
amplitude = fftshift(abs(fft(conj(pulseFunction(time)))))*dt;
end

%this function transforms a spectral distrubution into a temporal signal
function [signal] = Fourier2Time(time,amplitude)

dt = (time(end)-time(1))/length(time);
signal = conj(fftshift((ifft(ifftshift(conj(amplitude)))))).*(1/dt);

SplitOperatorPropagation()
%Propagate a wave packet in a time dependent and/or independent potential
%position = 1d spacial vector
%time = vector of times
%psiInit = form of the initial wave packet
%staticV = static potential
%dynamicV = driving potential function
%molDipole = molecular dipole function
%intervalTime = size of time interval for saving snapshots
%m = particle mass
function [timeSave,psiSave,totalVSave] =...
SplitOperatorPropagation(position,time,psiInit,staticV,dynamicV,...
molDipole,intervalTime,m)
%specify physical constants
hbar = 1;
%construct time vectors
stepsTime = length(time);
dt = time(2)-time(1);
%construct kinetic energy matrix in p space
182
==PAGE:375==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
stepsPosition = length(position);
dK = (2*pi)/(position(2)-position(1));
T_ind = (1/stepsPosition).*[(0:stepsPosition/2),(-(stepsPosition/2)+1:-1)];
T_k = (((hbarˆ2)/(2*m)).*(T_ind.*dK).ˆ2);
%if we only need the last value, use this loop:
if isempty(intervalTime)
psiSave(:,1) = psiInit;
totalVSave(:,1) = staticV;
facKin = exp(-i*((dt)/hbar).*T_k)’;
firstPsi = psiInit;
if or(isempty(dynamicV),isempty(molDipole))
for n = 1:stepsTime
totalV = staticV;
facPot = exp(-i*((dt)/(2*hbar)).*totalV)’;
secondPsi = facPot.*fft(facKin.*ifft(facPot.*firstPsi));
firstPsi = secondPsi;
end
else

firstPsi = secondPsi;
end
end
totalVSave = staticV;
psiSave = firstPsi;
timeSave = time(end);
else
saveIndex = [1,[intervalTime:intervalTime:stepsTime]];
psiSave = zeros(stepsPosition,length(saveIndex));
totalVSave = zeros(stepsPosition,length(saveIndex));
psiSave(:,1) = psiInit;
totalVSave(:,1) = staticV;

firstPsi = psiInit;

APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
M.15
HarmonicEigenstates()
%This function calculates the analytical expressions for the eigenstates
%and energies of a quantum harmonic oscillator
function
[eigPsi,eigEvec] = HarmonicEigenstates(position,harmPot,nStates)
hbar = 1;
omega = harmPot.omega;
m = harmPot.m;
stepsPosition = length(position);
n=[0:nStates];
n_mat = repmat(n,stepsPosition,1);
x_mat = repmat(position’,1,nStates+1);
eigPsi = (1./(sqrt(2.ˆn_mat.*factorial(n_mat)))).*...
(((m*omega)/(pi*hbar))ˆ(1/4)).*exp(-((m*omega)/(2*hbar)).*...
x_mat.ˆ2).*hermiteH(n_mat,sqrt(((m*omega)/(hbar))).*x_mat);
eigEvec = (hbar*omega.*(n+(1/2)))’;
%normalize Psi
dx = position(2)-position(1);
norm = sqrt(1/(trapz(abs(eigPsi(:,1)).ˆ2)*dx));
eigPsi = eigPsi*norm;
end

M.16
MorseEigenstates()
%calculate eigenstates and eigenenergies of Morse Potential
function [eigPsi,eigEvec] = MorseEigenstates(position,morsePot)
hbar = 1;
xmin = position(1);
xmax = position(end);
Nx = length(position);
De = morsePot.De;
a = morsePot.a;
re = morsePot.re;
m = morsePot.m;
%Calculate analytical eigenfunctions and energies
h = 2*pi*hbar;
v0 = (a/(2*pi))*sqrt((2*De)/m);
n_max = floor((2*De-h*v0)/(h*v0));
r = linspace(xmin,xmax,Nx);
n = [0:n_max];
n_mat = repmat(n,length(r),1)’;
lambda = (sqrt(2*m*De))/(a*hbar);
188
==PAGE:381==
APPENDIX M. MATLAB CODES
x_e = a*re;
alpha = 2*lambda-2.*n_mat-1;
x = repmat(a.*r,size(n_mat,1),1);
z = 2.*lambda*exp(-(x-x_e));
N = factorial(n_mat).*((2*lambda-2.*n_mat-1)./(gamma(n_mat+1).*...
gamma(2*lambda-n_mat))).ˆ(1/2);
eigPsi = ((N.*(z.ˆ(lambda-n_mat-1/2)).*exp(-(1/2)*z).*...
laguerreL(n_mat,alpha,z)).*sqrt(a*(r(2)-r(1))))’;
%normalize Psi
dx = position(2)-position(1);
norm = sqrt(1/(trapz(abs(eigPsi(:,1)).ˆ2)*dx));
eigPsi = eigPsi*norm;
%calculate eigenenergies
epsilon_n = -(lambda-n-(1/2)).ˆ2;
eigEvec = ((aˆ2*hbarˆ2)/(2*m).*epsilon_n)’;
end

function [eigPsi,eigEvec] = NumericEigenstates(position,staticV,m,nStates)

dx = (x(end)-x(1))/length(x);
i = repmat([1:N],N,1);
j = repmat([1:N],N,1)’;
H = zeros(N,N);
for l = 1:n
H = H + (2/N)*(cos((l*(2*pi).*(i-j))./N).*...
((2/m)*(((hbar*pi*l)./(N*dx))ˆ2)));
